    16 
    17 export interface EditorContentRef {
    18   getElement: () => HTMLDivElement | null;
    19   focus: () => void;
    20 }
    21 
    22 export const EditorContent = forwardRef<EditorContentRef, EditorContentProps>(
    23   ({ content, onChange, opacity, onSelectionChange, enableGlassEffect = false, glassBlur = 10, useBlackMask = false, onEditLink, onEditImage }, ref) => {
    24     const editorRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
    25 
    26     useImperativeHandle(ref, () => ({
    27       getElement: () => editorRef.current,
    28       focus: () => editorRef.current?.focus(),
    29     }));
    30 
    31     useEffect(() => {
    32       if (editorRef.current && editorRef.current.innerHTML !== content) {
    33         const selection = window.getSelection();
    34         const range = selection?.rangeCount ? selection.getRangeAt(0) : null;
    35         
    36         editorRef.current.innerHTML = content;
    37         
    38         if (range) {
    39           try {
    40             selection?.removeAllRanges();
    41             selection?.addRange(range);
    42           } catch (e) {
    43             // 忽略范围错误
    44           }
    45         }
    46       }
    47     }, [content]);
    48 
    49     const handleInput = () => {
    50       if (editorRef.current) {
    51         onChange(editorRef.current.innerHTML);
    52       }
    53     };
    54 
    55     const handlePaste = (e: React.ClipboardEvent) => {
    56       e.preventDefault();
    57       const text = e.clipboardData.getData('text/plain');
    58       document.execCommand('insertText', false, text);
    59     };
    60 
    61     const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    62       // Tab键：增加缩进
    63       if (e.key === 'Tab' && !e.shiftKey) {
    64         e.preventDefault();
    65         document.execCommand('indent', false);
    66       }
    67       // Shift+Tab：减少缩进
    68       else if (e.key === 'Tab' && e.shiftKey) {
    69         e.preventDefault();
    70         document.execCommand('outdent', false);
    71       }
    72     };
    73 
    74     const handleDoubleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    75       const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
    76       if (target.tagName === 'IMG' && onEditImage) {
    77         onEditImage(target as HTMLImageElement);
    78       }
    79     };
    80 
    81     const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    82       const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
    83       
    84       // 如果点击的是图片,选中它
    85       if (target.tagName === 'IMG') {
    86         const selection = window.getSelection();
    87         const range = document.createRange();
    88         range.selectNode(target);
    89         selection?.removeAllRanges();
    90         selection?.addRange(range);
    91       }
    92       
    93       // 如果点击的是链接编辑图标
    94       if (target.classList.contains('link-edit-icon')) {
    95         e.preventDefault();
    96         e.stopPropagation();
    97         
    98         // 找到父容器span，然后找到其中的a元素
    99         const parentSpan = target.parentElement;
   100         const linkElement = parentSpan?.querySelector('a') as HTMLAnchorElement;
   101         if (linkElement && onEditLink) {
   102           onEditLink(linkElement);
   103         }
   104       }
   105       
   106       // 如果点击的是卡片编辑按钮
   107       if (target.classList.contains('card-edit-btn')) {
   108         e.preventDefault();
   109         e.stopPropagation();
   110         
   111         // 找到卡片元素
   112         const cardElement = target.closest('.link-card') as HTMLElement;
   113         if (cardElement && onEditLink) {
   114           // 将卡片元素作为特殊的"链接"传递
   115           onEditLink(cardElement as unknown as HTMLAnchorElement);
   116         }
   117       }
   118     };
   119 
   120     // 根据useBlackMask设置决定使用黑色还是白色背景
   121     const backgroundColor = useBlackMask 
   122       ? `rgba(0, 0, 0, ${opacity / 100})`
   123       : `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${opacity / 100})`;
   124     const textColor = useBlackMask ? '#ffffff' : undefined;
   125 
   126     return (
   127       <div className="flex justify-center py-6 relative">
   128         {/* 文档纸张容器 */}
   129         <div 
   130           className={cn(
   131             "w-full max-w-[21cm] shadow-xl rounded-2xl overflow-hidden hover-lift transition-all duration-300",
   132             !enableGlassEffect && !useBlackMask && opacity === 100 && "bg-card"
   133           )}
   134           style={{
   135             minHeight: '29.7cm',
   136             background: enableGlassEffect ? 'transparent' : backgroundColor,
   137             backdropFilter: enableGlassEffect ? `blur(${glassBlur}px)` : (opacity < 100 ? 'blur(8px)' : 'none')
   138           }}
   139         >
   140           {/* 可编辑内容区域 */}
   141           <div
   142             ref={editorRef}
   143             contentEditable
   144             onInput={handleInput}
   145             onPaste={handlePaste}
   146             onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
   147             onClick={handleClick}
   148             onDoubleClick={handleDoubleClick}
   149             className="min-h-[29.7cm] p-8 md:p-12 lg:p-16 focus:outline-none editor-content relative transition-smooth"
   150             style={{
   151               backgroundColor,
   152               color: textColor,
   153               backdropFilter: enableGlassEffect ? `blur(${glassBlur}px)` : 'none',
   154               WebkitBackdropFilter: enableGlassEffect ? `blur(${glassBlur}px)` : 'none',
   155               fontSize: '15px',
   156               lineHeight: '1.8',
   157               fontFamily: '-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Segoe UI", "Microsoft YaHei", "PingFang SC", sans-serif',
   158             }}
   159             onMouseUp={onSelectionChange}
   160             onKeyUp={onSelectionChange}
   161             suppressContentEditableWarning
   162           />
   163         </div>
   164         
   165         <style>{`
   166           .editor-content a {
   167             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#60a5fa' : '#4361ee'};
   168             text-decoration: underline;
   169             cursor: pointer;
   170           }
   171           
   172           .editor-content a:hover {
   173             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#93c5fd' : '#3f37c9'};
   174           }
   175           
   176           .editor-content .link-edit-icon {
   177             text-decoration: none !important;
   178             user-select: none;
   179             -webkit-user-select: none;
   180             -moz-user-select: none;
   181             -ms-user-select: none;
   182             pointer-events: auto;
   183           }
   184           
   185           .editor-content .link-wrapper:hover .link-edit-icon {
   186             opacity: 1 !important;
   187           }
   188           
   189           .editor-content h1 {
   190             font-size: 2em;
   191             font-weight: bold;
   192             margin-top: 0.5em;
   193             margin-bottom: 0.5em;
   194             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#60a5fa' : '#4361ee'};
   195           }
   196           
   197           .editor-content h2 {
   198             font-size: 1.5em;
   199             font-weight: bold;
   200             margin-top: 0.6em;
   201             margin-bottom: 0.6em;
   202             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#60a5fa' : '#4361ee'};
   203           }
   204           
   205           .editor-content h3 {
   206             font-size: 1.17em;
   207             font-weight: bold;
   208             margin-top: 0.7em;
   209             margin-bottom: 0.7em;
   210             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#60a5fa' : '#4361ee'};
   211           }
   212           
   213           .editor-content h4 {
   214             font-size: 1em;
   215             font-weight: bold;
   216             margin-top: 0.8em;
   217             margin-bottom: 0.8em;
   218             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#60a5fa' : '#4361ee'};
   219           }
   220           
   221           .editor-content h5 {
   222             font-size: 0.83em;
   223             font-weight: bold;
   224             margin-top: 0.9em;
   225             margin-bottom: 0.9em;
   226             color: ${useBlackMask ? '#60a5fa' : '#4361ee'};
   227           }
   228           
   229           .editor-content h6 {
   230             font-size: 0.67em;
   231             font-weight: bold;

   236

AgentThinkAction(thought='\n用户报告了一个 JavaScript 语法错误："Uncaught SyntaxError: Invalid left-hand side in assignment"。这个错误通常发生在赋值语句的左侧不是一个有效的左值时。\n\n让我分析可能的原因：\n\n1. 在导出的 HTML 中，我看到了这行代码：\n```javascript\nwhile(node = walk.nextNode()) textNodes.push(node);\n```\n\n这是一个常见的模式，在 while 循环中进行赋值并检查结果。这在 JavaScript 中是合法的。\n\n2. 另一个可能的问题是：\n```javascript\ndocument.getElementById(\'attachOpenBtn\').onclick = function() {\n```\n\n这也是合法的。\n\n3. 还有一个可能的问题：\n```javascript\n<button class="scroll-btn" onclick="(function(){var mc=document.getElementById(\'mainContainer\');mc.scrollTo({top:mc.scrollHeight,behavior:\'smooth\'});})()" title="跳到底部">\n```\n\n这里使用了立即执行函数表达式 (IIFE)，语法看起来是正确的。\n\n等等，我注意到一个问题！在 onclick 属性中使用 IIFE 时，最后的 `()` 会立即执行函数，但这不是我们想要的。onclick 应该是一个函数引用或函数调用，而不是 IIFE 的执行结果。\n\n让我检查这行代码：\n```html\n<button class="scroll-btn" onclick="(function(){var mc=document.getElementById(\'mainContainer\');mc.scrollTo({top:mc.scrollHeight,behavior:\'smooth\'});})()" title="跳到底部">\n```\n\n这里的问题是：`(function(){...})()` 是一个 IIFE，它会立即执行并返回 undefined。但是在 onclick 属性中，我们需要的是一个函数调用，而不是 IIFE。\n\n正确的写法应该是：\n```html\n<button class="scroll-btn" onclick="(function(){var mc=document.getElementById(\'mainContainer\');mc.scrollTo({top:mc.scrollHeight,behavior:\'smooth\'});})();" title="跳到底部">\n```\n\n或者更简单的：\n```html\n<button class="scroll-btn" onclick="var mc=document.getElementById(\'mainContainer\');mc.scrollTo({top:mc.scrollHeight,behavior:\'smooth\'});" title="跳到底部">\n```\n\n或者定义一个函数：\n```html\n<button class="scroll-btn" onclick="scrollToBottom()" title="跳到底部">\n```\n\n然后在 script 中定义：\n```javascript\nfunction scrollToBottom() {\n  var mc = document.getElementById(\'mainContainer\');\n  mc.scrollTo({top: mc.scrollHeight, behavior: \'smooth\'});\n}\n```\n\n我认为最简单的解决方案是直接在 onclick 中写代码，不使用 IIFE。\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)
</action>

New String: ```
    // 附件查看功能
    function viewAttachment(id) {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (!el) return;
      const dataStr = el.getAttribute('data-attachment');
      const data = JSON.parse(dataStr);
      if (data.code) {
        document.getElementById('attachFileName').innerText = '附件 ' + data.name + ' 需要提取码。';
        document.getElementById('attachCodeInput').value = data.code;
        document.getElementById('attachmentDialog').classList.add('active');
        document.getElementById('attachOpenBtn').onclick = function() {
          copyAttachCode();
          window.open(data.url, '_blank');
          closeAttachDialog();
        };
      } else {
        window.open(data.url, '_blank');
      }
    }
    
    function closeAttachDialog() {
      document.getElementById('attachmentDialog').classList.remove('active');
    }
    
    function copyAttachCode() {
      const input = document.getElementById('attachCodeInput');
      input.select();
      document.execCommand('copy');
      // 可以选择是否 alert，在离线环境下 alert 比较保险
      alert('提取码已复制');
    }

    function scrollToTop() {
      const mc = document.getElementById('mainContainer');
      if (mc) mc.scrollTo({top: 0, behavior: 'smooth'});
    }
    
    function scrollToBottom() {
      const mc = document.getElementById('mainContainer');
      if (mc) mc.scrollTo({top: mc.scrollHeight, behavior: 'smooth'});
    }

    // 图片查看器功能
```

  3161     function saveCollapseState() {

  3287     function performSearch(keyword) {
  3288       const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
  3289       
  3290       if (!keyword) {

  3292         document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(wrapper => {
  3293           wrapper.innerHTML = originalContents[wrapper.id];

  3300       }
  3301 
  3302       const regex = new RegExp('(' + keyword.replace(/[.*+?^\${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
  3303       let firstMatchPageId = null;
  3304 
  3305       document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(wrapper => {
  3306         const originalHtml = originalContents[wrapper.id];
  3307         const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
  3308         tempDiv.innerHTML = originalHtml;
  3309         
  3310         // 深度优先遍历文本节点进行高亮，避开标签属性
  3311         const textNodes = [];
  3312         const walk = document.createTreeWalker(tempDiv, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, null, false);
  3313         let node = walk.nextNode();
  3314         while(node) {
  3315           textNodes.push(node);
  3316           node = walk.nextNode();
  3317         }
  3318 
  3319         let hasMatch = false;
  3320         textNodes.forEach(node => {
  3321           if (node.nodeValue.match(regex)) {
  3322             hasMatch = true;
  3323             const parent = node.parentNode;
  3324             if (parent && parent.tagName !== 'SCRIPT' && parent.tagName !== 'STYLE') {
  3325               const span = document.createElement('span');
  3326               span.innerHTML = node.nodeValue.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
  3327               parent.replaceChild(span, node);
  3328             }
  3329           }
  3330         });
  3331 
  3332         wrapper.innerHTML = tempDiv.innerHTML;
  3333         
  3334         // 更新侧边栏项显示状态
  3335         const pageId = wrapper.id;
  3336         const sidebarItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
  3337         
  3338         // 如果页面内容匹配，或者标题匹配
  3339         const titleMatch = sidebarItem && sidebarItem.querySelector('.title').textContent.match(regex);
  3340         
  3341         if (hasMatch || titleMatch) {
  3342           // 显示当前项及其所有父项
  3343           if (sidebarItem) {
  3344             let current = sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group');
  3345             while (current) {
  3346               current.style.display = 'block';
  3347               const parentSubItems = current.parentElement.closest('.sidebar-sub-items');
  3348               current = parentSubItems ? parentSubItems.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
  3349             }
  3350           }
  3351           if (!firstMatchPageId) firstMatchPageId = pageId;
  3352           
  3353           // 如果是标题匹配，高亮侧边栏标题
  3354           if (titleMatch && sidebarItem) {
  3355             const titleEl = sidebarItem.querySelector('.title');
  3356             titleEl.innerHTML = titleEl.textContent.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
  3357           }
  3358         } else {
  3359           // 暂时隐藏
  3360           const sidebarGroup = sidebarItem ? sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
  3361           if (sidebarGroup) sidebarGroup.style.display = 'none';
  3362         }
  3363       });

  3366       if (firstMatchPageId) {

  3369     }

```
    function initSearch() {
      var searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
      if (!searchInput) return;

      // 存储原始 HTML 内容以便恢复
      document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(function(wrapper) {
        originalContents[wrapper.id] = wrapper.innerHTML;
      });

      searchInput.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
        clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
        searchTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
          performSearch(e.target.value.trim());
        }, 300);
```

```
      document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(wrapper => {
        const originalHtml = originalContents[wrapper.id];
        const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
        tempDiv.innerHTML = originalHtml;
        
        // 深度优先遍历文本节点进行高亮，避开标签属性
        const textNodes = [];
        const walk = document.createTreeWalker(tempDiv, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, null, false);
        let node = walk.nextNode();
        while(node) {
          textNodes.push(node);
          node = walk.nextNode();
        }

        let hasMatch = false;
        textNodes.forEach(node => {
          if (node.nodeValue.match(regex)) {
            hasMatch = true;
            const parent = node.parentNode;
            if (parent && parent.tagName !== 'SCRIPT' && parent.tagName !== 'STYLE') {
              const span = document.createElement('span');
              span.innerHTML = node.nodeValue.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
              parent.replaceChild(span, node);
            }
          }
        });

        wrapper.innerHTML = tempDiv.innerHTML;

        const pageId = wrapper.id;
        const sidebarItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');

        const titleMatch = sidebarItem && sidebarItem.querySelector('.title').textContent.match(regex);

          // 显示当前项及其所有父项

              current.style.display = 'block';
              const parentSubItems = current.parentElement.closest('.sidebar-sub-items');
              current = parentSubItems ? parentSubItems.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;

          if (!firstMatchPageId) firstMatchPageId = pageId;

            titleEl.innerHTML = titleEl.textContent.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');

        } else {
          // 暂时隐藏
          const sidebarGroup = sidebarItem ? sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
          if (sidebarGroup) sidebarGroup.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });
```

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bc81t9sadtdt/src/pages/Editor.tsx]
Thought: 
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
    // ── 折叠状态 localStorage 工具 ──────────────────────────────
    // key 包含文档标题，避免不同导出文件互相覆盖
    const COLLAPSE_KEY = 'sidebar-collapse:' + document.title;

    function saveCollapseState() {
      const expanded = [];
      document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-sub-items').forEach(function(el) {
        if (el.style.display !== 'none') {
          // 找到对应的父级 anchor 的 data-id
          const group = el.parentElement;
          if (group) {
            const anchor = group.querySelector(':scope > a.sidebar-item');
            if (anchor && anchor.getAttribute('data-id')) {
              expanded.push(anchor.getAttribute('data-id'));
            }
          }
        }
      });
      try { localStorage.setItem(COLLAPSE_KEY, JSON.stringify(expanded)); } catch(e) {}
    }

    function restoreCollapseState() {
      let expanded = [];
      try { expanded = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(COLLAPSE_KEY) || '[]'); } catch(e) {}
      if (!Array.isArray(expanded) || expanded.length === 0) return;
      expanded.forEach(function(pageId) {
        const anchor = document.querySelector('a.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
        if (!anchor) return;
        const group = anchor.parentElement;
        if (!group) return;
        for (let i = 0; i < group.children.length; i++) {
          if (group.children[i].classList.contains('sidebar-sub-items')) {
            group.children[i].style.display = 'block';
            break;
          }
        }
        const arrow = anchor.querySelector('.toggle-arrow');
        if (arrow && !arrow.classList.contains('invisible')) {
          arrow.textContent = '▼';
          arrow.classList.add('expanded');
        }
      });
    }
```
New String: ```
    // ── 折叠状态 localStorage 工具 ──────────────────────────────
    // key 包含文档标题，避免不同导出文件互相覆盖
    var COLLAPSE_KEY = 'sidebar-collapse:' + document.title;

    function saveCollapseState() {
      var expanded = [];
      var sidebarSubItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-sub-items');
      for (var i = 0; i < sidebarSubItems.length; i++) {
        var el = sidebarSubItems[i];
        if (el.style.display !== 'none') {
          // 找到对应的父级 anchor 的 data-id
          var group = el.parentElement;
          if (group) {
            var anchor = group.querySelector(':scope > a.sidebar-item');
            if (anchor && anchor.getAttribute('data-id')) {
              expanded.push(anchor.getAttribute('data-id'));
            }
          }
        }
      }
      try { localStorage.setItem(COLLAPSE_KEY, JSON.stringify(expanded)); } catch(e) {}
    }

    function restoreCollapseState() {
      var expanded = [];
      try { expanded = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(COLLAPSE_KEY) || '[]'); } catch(e) {}
      if (!Array.isArray(expanded) || expanded.length === 0) return;
      for (var j = 0; j < expanded.length; j++) {
        (function(pageId) {
          var anchor = document.querySelector('a.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
          if (!anchor) return;
          var group = anchor.parentElement;
          if (!group) return;
          for (var i = 0; i < group.children.length; i++) {
            if (group.children[i].classList.contains('sidebar-sub-items')) {
              group.children[i].style.display = 'block';
              break;
            }
          }
          var arrow = anchor.querySelector('.toggle-arrow');
          if (arrow && !arrow.classList.contains('invisible')) {
            arrow.textContent = '▼';
            arrow.classList.add('expanded');
          }
        })(expanded[j]);
      }
    }
```

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bc81t9sadtdt/src/pages/Editor.tsx]
Thought: 
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
      // 侧边栏拖拽调整宽度
      const resizer = document.getElementById('sidebarResizer');
      const sidebar = document.querySelector('.sidebar');
      const MIN_WIDTH = 120;
      const MAX_WIDTH = 600;
      let isResizing = false;
      let startX = 0;
      let startWidth = 0;

      // 从 localStorage 恢复上次拖拽宽度（优先于 CSS 变量初始宽度）
      const savedWidth = localStorage.getItem('sidebar-width');
      if (savedWidth && sidebar) {
        const w = parseInt(savedWidth, 10);
        if (w >= MIN_WIDTH && w <= MAX_WIDTH) {
          sidebar.style.width = w + 'px';
        }
      }

      if (resizer && sidebar) {
        resizer.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
          isResizing = true;
          startX = e.clientX;
          startWidth = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(sidebar).width, 10);
          resizer.classList.add('dragging');
          document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
          document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
        });

        document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
          if (!isResizing || !sidebar) return;
          const delta = e.clientX - startX;
          const newWidth = Math.max(MIN_WIDTH, Math.min(MAX_WIDTH, startWidth + delta));
          sidebar.style.width = newWidth + 'px';
        });

        document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
          if (isResizing) {
            isResizing = false;
            resizer.classList.remove('dragging');
            document.body.style.cursor = '';
            document.body.style.userSelect = '';
            if (sidebar) {
              localStorage.setItem('sidebar-width', sidebar.style.width.replace('px', ''));
            }
          }
        });
      }
```
New String: ```
      // 侧边栏拖拽调整宽度
      var resizer = document.getElementById('sidebarResizer');
      var sidebar = document.querySelector('.sidebar');
      var MIN_WIDTH = 120;
      var MAX_WIDTH = 600;
      var isResizing = false;
      var startX = 0;
      var startWidth = 0;

      // 从 localStorage 恢复上次拖拽宽度（优先于 CSS 变量初始宽度）
      var savedWidth = localStorage.getItem('sidebar-width');
      if (savedWidth && sidebar) {
        var w = parseInt(savedWidth, 10);
        if (w >= MIN_WIDTH && w <= MAX_WIDTH) {
          sidebar.style.width = w + 'px';
        }
      }

      if (resizer && sidebar) {
        resizer.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
          isResizing = true;
          startX = e.clientX;
          startWidth = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(sidebar).width, 10);
          resizer.classList.add('dragging');
          document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
          document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
        });

        document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
          if (!isResizing || !sidebar) return;
          var delta = e.clientX - startX;
          var newWidth = Math.max(MIN_WIDTH, Math.min(MAX_WIDTH, startWidth + delta));
          sidebar.style.width = newWidth + 'px';
        });

        document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
          if (isResizing) {
            isResizing = false;
            if (resizer) resizer.classList.remove('dragging');
            document.body.style.cursor = '';
            document.body.style.userSelect = '';
            if (sidebar) {
              localStorage.setItem('sidebar-width', sidebar.style.width.replace('px', ''));
            }
          }
        });
      }
```

Old String: ```
      // 侧边栏拖拽调整宽度
      const resizer = document.getElementById('sidebarResizer');
      const sidebar = document.querySelector('.sidebar');
      const MIN_WIDTH = 120;
      const MAX_WIDTH = 600;
      let isResizing = false;
      let startX = 0;
      let startWidth = 0;

      // 从 localStorage 恢复上次拖拽宽度（优先于 CSS 变量初始宽度）
      const savedWidth = localStorage.getItem('sidebar-width');
      if (savedWidth && sidebar) {
        const w = parseInt(savedWidth, 10);
        if (w >= MIN_WIDTH && w <= MAX_WIDTH) {
          sidebar.style.width = w + 'px';
        }
      }

      if (resizer && sidebar) {
        resizer.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
          isResizing = true;
          startX = e.clientX;
          startWidth = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(sidebar).width, 10);
          resizer.classList.add('dragging');
          document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
          document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
        });
      }
```

```
      document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
        if (!isResizing || !sidebar) return;
```
```
        const delta = e.clientX - startX;
        const newWidth = Math.max(MIN_WIDTH, Math.min(MAX_WIDTH, startWidth + delta));
        sidebar.style.width = newWidth + 'px';
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
        if (!isResizing || !sidebar) return;
        isResizing = false;
        resizer.classList.remove('dragging');
        document.body.style.cursor = '';
        document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        localStorage.setItem('sidebar-width', sidebar.style.width.replace('px', ''));
      });
```

```
        var w = parseInt(savedWidth, 10);

          sidebar.style.width = w + 'px';
        }
      }

      if (resizer && sidebar) {
        resizer.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
          isResizing = true;
          startX = e.clientX;
          startWidth = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(sidebar).width, 10);
          resizer.classList.add('dragging');
          document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
          document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
        });
      }

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
        if (!isResizing || !sidebar) return;
        var delta = e.clientX - startX;
        var newWidth = Math.max(MIN_WIDTH, Math.min(MAX_WIDTH, startWidth + delta));
        sidebar.style.width = newWidth + 'px';
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
        if (!isResizing || !sidebar) return;
        isResizing = false;
        if (resizer) resizer.classList.remove('dragging');
        document.body.style.cursor = '';
        document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        localStorage.setItem('sidebar-width', sidebar.style.width.replace('px', ''));
      });
```

```
    // 侧边栏高亮与页面切换

      if (typeof pageId === 'string' && !pageId.startsWith('page-')) {
        pageId = 'page-' + pageId;
      }
      
      // 移除所有 active 类
      document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item').forEach(function(el) {
        el.classList.remove('active');

        activeItem.classList.add('active');
```

New String: ```
    function switchPage(pageId) {
      if (typeof pageId === 'string' && !pageId.startsWith('page-')) {
        pageId = 'page-' + pageId;
      }
      
      // 移除所有 active 类
      var sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
      for (var i = 0; i < sidebarItems.length; i++) {
        sidebarItems[i].classList.remove('active');
      }
      
      // 隐藏所有页面内容
      var pageWrappers = document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper');
      for (var j = 0; j < pageWrappers.length; j++) {
        pageWrappers[j].style.display = 'none';
      }
      
      // 为当前项添加 active 类，展开祖先，滚动到可见
      var activeItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
      if (activeItem) {
        activeItem.classList.add('active');
        expandAncestors(pageId);
        activeItem.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
      }
      
      // 显示当前页面内容
      var activePage = document.getElementById(pageId);
      if (activePage) {
        activePage.style.display = 'block';
      }
    }
```

```
    function initSearch() {
      var searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
      if (!searchInput) return;

      // 存储原始 HTML 内容以便恢复

      searchInput.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
```

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bc81t9sadtdt/src/pages/Editor.tsx]
Thought: 
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
    function performSearch(keyword) {
      var sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
      
      if (!keyword) {
        // 恢复原始内容
        document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(function(wrapper) {
          wrapper.innerHTML = originalContents[wrapper.id];
        });
        // 显示所有侧边栏项
        document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item-group').forEach(function(group) {
          group.style.display = 'block';
        });
        return;
      }

      var regex = new RegExp('(' + keyword.replace(/[.*+?^\${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
      var firstMatchPageId = null;

      document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(function(wrapper) {
        var originalHtml = originalContents[wrapper.id];
        var tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
        tempDiv.innerHTML = originalHtml;
        
        // 深度优先遍历文本节点进行高亮，避开标签属性
        var textNodes = [];
        var walk = document.createTreeWalker(tempDiv, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, null, false);
        var node = walk.nextNode();
        while(node) {
          textNodes.push(node);
          node = walk.nextNode();
        }

        var hasMatch = false;
        textNodes.forEach(function(node) {
          if (node.nodeValue.match(regex)) {
            hasMatch = true;
            var parent = node.parentNode;
            if (parent && parent.tagName !== 'SCRIPT' && parent.tagName !== 'STYLE') {
              var span = document.createElement('span');
              span.innerHTML = node.nodeValue.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
              parent.replaceChild(span, node);
            }
          }
        });

        wrapper.innerHTML = tempDiv.innerHTML;
        
        // 更新侧边栏项显示状态
        var pageId = wrapper.id;
        var sidebarItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
        
        // 如果页面内容匹配，或者标题匹配
        var titleMatch = sidebarItem && sidebarItem.querySelector('.title').textContent.match(regex);
        
        if (hasMatch || titleMatch) {
          // 显示当前项及其所有父项
          if (sidebarItem) {
            var current = sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group');
            while (current) {
              current.style.display = 'block';
              var parentSubItems = current.parentElement.closest('.sidebar-sub-items');
              current = parentSubItems ? parentSubItems.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
            }
          }
          if (!firstMatchPageId) firstMatchPageId = pageId;
          
          // 如果是标题匹配，高亮侧边栏标题
          if (titleMatch && sidebarItem) {
            var titleEl = sidebarItem.querySelector('.title');
            titleEl.innerHTML = titleEl.textContent.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
          }
        } else {
          // 暂时隐藏
          var sidebarGroup = sidebarItem ? sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
          if (sidebarGroup) sidebarGroup.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });

      // 如果有匹配结果，切换到第一个匹配页面
      if (firstMatchPageId) {
        switchPage(firstMatchPageId);
      }
    }
```
New String: ```
    function performSearch(keyword) {
      var sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
      
      if (!keyword) {
        // 恢复原始内容
        var wrappers = document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper');
        for (var i = 0; i < wrappers.length; i++) {
          var wrapper = wrappers[i];
          wrapper.innerHTML = originalContents[wrapper.id];
        }
        // 显示所有侧边栏项
        var groups = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item-group');
        for (var j = 0; j < groups.length; j++) {
          groups[j].style.display = 'block';
        }
        return;
      }

      var regex = new RegExp('(' + keyword.replace(/[.*+?^\${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
      var firstMatchPageId = null;

      var allWrappers = document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper');
      for (var k = 0; k < allWrappers.length; k++) {
        (function(wrapper) {
          var originalHtml = originalContents[wrapper.id];
          var tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
          tempDiv.innerHTML = originalHtml;
          
          // 深度优先遍历文本节点进行高亮，避开标签属性
          var textNodes = [];
          var walk = document.createTreeWalker(tempDiv, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, null, false);
          var node = walk.nextNode();
          while(node) {
            textNodes.push(node);
            node = walk.nextNode();
          }

          var hasMatch = false;
          for (var m = 0; m < textNodes.length; m++) {
            var textNode = textNodes[m];
            if (textNode.nodeValue.match(regex)) {
              hasMatch = true;
              var parent = textNode.parentNode;
              if (parent && parent.tagName !== 'SCRIPT' && parent.tagName !== 'STYLE') {
                var span = document.createElement('span');
                span.innerHTML = textNode.nodeValue.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
                parent.replaceChild(span, textNode);
              }
            }
          }

          wrapper.innerHTML = tempDiv.innerHTML;
          
          // 更新侧边栏项显示状态
          var pageId = wrapper.id;
          var sidebarItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
          
          // 如果页面内容匹配，或者标题匹配
          var titleMatch = sidebarItem && sidebarItem.querySelector('.title').textContent.match(regex);
          
          if (hasMatch || titleMatch) {
            // 显示当前项及其所有父项
            if (sidebarItem) {
              var current = sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group');
              while (current) {
                current.style.display = 'block';
                var parentSubItems = current.parentElement.closest('.sidebar-sub-items');
                current = parentSubItems ? parentSubItems.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
              }
            }
            if (!firstMatchPageId) firstMatchPageId = pageId;
            
            // 如果是标题匹配，高亮侧边栏标题
            if (titleMatch && sidebarItem) {
              var titleEl = sidebarItem.querySelector('.title');
              titleEl.innerHTML = titleEl.textContent.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
            }
          } else {
            // 暂时隐藏
            var sidebarGroup = sidebarItem ? sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
            if (sidebarGroup) sidebarGroup.style.display = 'none';
          }
        })(allWrappers[k]);
      }

      // 如果有匹配结果，切换到第一个匹配页面
      if (firstMatchPageId) {
        switchPage(firstMatchPageId);
      }
    }
```

```
    function performSearch(keyword) {
      const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
      
      if (!keyword) {
        // 恢复原始内容
        document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(wrapper => {
          wrapper.innerHTML = originalContents[wrapper.id];
        });
        // 显示所有侧边栏项
        document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item-group').forEach(group => {
          group.style.display = 'block';
        });
        return;
      }

      const regex = new RegExp('(' + keyword.replace(/[.*+?^\${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
      let firstMatchPageId = null;

      document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper').forEach(function(wrapper) {
        var originalHtml = originalContents[wrapper.id];
        var tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
        tempDiv.innerHTML = originalHtml;
        
        // 深度优先遍历文本节点进行高亮，避开标签属性
        var textNodes = [];
        var walk = document.createTreeWalker(tempDiv, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, null, false);
        var node = walk.nextNode();
        while(node) {
          textNodes.push(node);
          node = walk.nextNode();
        }

        var hasMatch = false;
        textNodes.forEach(function(node) {
          if (node.nodeValue.match(regex)) {
            hasMatch = true;
            var parent = node.parentNode;
            if (parent && parent.tagName !== 'SCRIPT' && parent.tagName !== 'STYLE') {
              var span = document.createElement('span');
              span.innerHTML = node.nodeValue.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
              parent.replaceChild(span, node);
            }
          }
        });

        wrapper.innerHTML = tempDiv.innerHTML;
        
        // 更新侧边栏项显示状态
        var pageId = wrapper.id;
        var sidebarItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
        
        // 如果页面内容匹配，或者标题匹配
        var titleMatch = sidebarItem && sidebarItem.querySelector('.title').textContent.match(regex);
        
        if (hasMatch || titleMatch) {
          // 显示当前项及其所有父项
          if (sidebarItem) {
            var current = sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group');
            while (current) {
              current.style.display = 'block';
              var parentSubItems = current.parentElement.closest('.sidebar-sub-items');
              current = parentSubItems ? parentSubItems.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
            }
          }
          if (!firstMatchPageId) firstMatchPageId = pageId;
          
          // 如果是标题匹配，高亮侧边栏标题
          if (titleMatch && sidebarItem) {
            var titleEl = sidebarItem.querySelector('.title');
            titleEl.innerHTML = titleEl.textContent.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
          }

          // 暂时隐藏
          var sidebarGroup = sidebarItem ? sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
          if (sidebarGroup) sidebarGroup.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });

      // 如果有匹配结果，切换到第一个匹配页面
      if (firstMatchPageId) {
        switchPage(firstMatchPageId);
```

New String: ```
    function performSearch(keyword) {
      var sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
      
      if (!keyword) {
        // 恢复原始内容
        var wrappers = document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper');
        for (var i = 0; i < wrappers.length; i++) {
          wrappers[i].innerHTML = originalContents[wrappers[i].id];
        }
        // 显示所有侧边栏项
        var groups = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item-group');
        for (var j = 0; j < groups.length; j++) {
          groups[j].style.display = 'block';
        }
        return;
      }

      var regex = new RegExp('(' + keyword.replace(/[.*+?^\${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
      var firstMatchPageId = null;

      var pageWrappers = document.querySelectorAll('.page-content-wrapper');
      for (var k = 0; k < pageWrappers.length; k++) {
        (function(wrapper) {
          var originalHtml = originalContents[wrapper.id];
          var tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
          tempDiv.innerHTML = originalHtml;
          
          // 深度优先遍历文本节点进行高亮，避开标签属性
          var textNodes = [];
          var walk = document.createTreeWalker(tempDiv, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, null, false);
          var node = walk.nextNode();
          while(node) {
            textNodes.push(node);
            node = walk.nextNode();
          }

          var hasMatch = false;
          for (var m = 0; m < textNodes.length; m++) {
            var textNode = textNodes[m];
            if (textNode.nodeValue.match(regex)) {
              hasMatch = true;
              var parent = textNode.parentNode;
              if (parent && parent.tagName !== 'SCRIPT' && parent.tagName !== 'STYLE') {
                var span = document.createElement('span');
                span.innerHTML = textNode.nodeValue.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
                parent.replaceChild(span, textNode);
              }
            }
          }

          wrapper.innerHTML = tempDiv.innerHTML;
          
          // 更新侧边栏项显示状态
          var pageId = wrapper.id;
          var sidebarItem = document.querySelector('.sidebar-item[data-id="' + pageId + '"]');
          
          // 如果页面内容匹配，或者标题匹配
          var titleMatch = sidebarItem && sidebarItem.querySelector('.title').textContent.match(regex);
          
          if (hasMatch || titleMatch) {
            // 显示当前项及其所有父项
            if (sidebarItem) {
              var current = sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group');
              while (current) {
                current.style.display = 'block';
                var parentSubItems = current.parentElement.closest('.sidebar-sub-items');
                current = parentSubItems ? parentSubItems.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
              }
            }
            if (!firstMatchPageId) firstMatchPageId = pageId;
            
            // 如果是标题匹配，高亮侧边栏标题
            if (titleMatch && sidebarItem) {
              var titleEl = sidebarItem.querySelector('.title');
              titleEl.innerHTML = titleEl.textContent.replace(regex, '<span class="search-result-highlight">$1</span>');
            }
          } else {
            // 暂时隐藏
            var sidebarGroup = sidebarItem ? sidebarItem.closest('.sidebar-item-group') : null;
            if (sidebarGroup) sidebarGroup.style.display = 'none';
          }
        })(pageWrappers[k]);
      }

      // 如果有匹配结果，切换到第一个匹配页面
      if (firstMatchPageId) {
        switchPage(firstMatchPageId);
      }
    }
```
